from flask import Flask, render_template, request, url_for, redirect
from scrapers import scrape_trendyol, scrape_hepsiburada  # ileride implemente edeceÄŸiz

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/", methods=["GET"])
def home():
    # Ana sayfa: arama formu
    return render_template("index.html")

@app.route("/search", methods=["POST"])
def search():
    # Formdan gelen Ã¼rÃ¼n adÄ±
    product_name = request.form.get("product_name", "").strip()
    if not product_name:
        return redirect(url_for("home"))

    # --- Burada gerÃ§ek scraper Ã§aÄŸrÄ±larÄ± olacak ---
    # Åimdilik 'mock' (Ã¶rnek) verilerle dÃ¶nÃ¼yoruz, scrapers.py'da implementasyonlar hazÄ±r olduÄŸunda deÄŸiÅŸecek.
    trendyol_result = scrape_trendyol(product_name)
    hepsi_result = scrape_hepsiburada(product_name)

    # sonuÃ§larÄ± bir listeye koy, en ucuzunu seÃ§mek kolay olsun
    results = [trendyol_result, hepsi_result]
    # None dÃ¶nebilir; filtrele
    results = [r for r in results if r is not None]

    # En dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼k fiyatÄ± bul (fiyat yoksa atla)
    cheapest = None
    for r in results:
        if r.get("price") is None:
            continue
        if cheapest is None or r["price"] < cheapest["price"]:
            cheapest = r

    return render_template(
        "results.html",
        query=product_name,
        results=results,
        cheapest=cheapest
    )

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(debug=True)
AÃ§Ä±klama:

/ â†’ ana sayfa (index.html) gÃ¶sterir.

/search â†’ POST ile gelen product_name alÄ±r, scraper fonksiyonlarÄ±na (ÅŸimdilik mock) sorar, sonuÃ§larÄ± results.html'e yollar.

from flask import Flask, render_template, request

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route("/")
def home():
    return render_template("index.html")


def fiyat_bul(model):
    fake_prices = [
        {"site": "Trendyol", "price": "24.999 TL", "link": "https://www.trendyol.com"},
        {"site": "Hepsiburada", "price": "25.299 TL", "link": "https://www.hepsiburada.com"},
        {"site": "N11", "price": "25.150 TL", "link": "https://www.n11.com"},
        {"site": "Amazon", "price": "25.000 TL", "link": "https://www.amazon.com/"},
    ]
    return fake_prices


@app.route("/search")
def search():
    model = request.args.get("model")

    fiyatlar = fiyat_bul(model)  # â† BURASI DÃœZELDÄ°

    # Ucuzdan pahalÄ±ya sÄ±ralama
    fiyatlar.sort(key=lambda x: float(x["price"].replace(".", "").replace(",", ".").split()[0]))

    return render_template("search_results.html", model=model, fiyatlar=fiyatlar)


@app.route("/about")
def about():
    return render_template("about.html")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(debug=True)

    return render_template("index.html")

def fiyat_bul(model):
    fake_prices = [
        {"site": "Trendyol", "price": "24.999 TL", "link": "https://www.trendyol.com"},

def get_prices(model):

    fake_prices = [
        {"site": "Trendyol", "price": "24.999 TL", "link": "https://www.trendyol.com"},
        {"site": "Hepsiburada", "price": "25.299 TL", "link": "https://www.hepsiburada.com"},
        {"site": "N11", "price": "25.150 TL", "link": "https://www.n11.com"},

def parse_price(price_str):
    # Ã–rn: "24.999 TL" -> 24999.0
    s = price_str.split()[0]             # "24.999"
    s = s.replace(".", "").replace(",", ".")
    try:
        return float(s)
    except:
        return float('inf')

@app.route("/search")
def search():
    model = request.args.get("model", "")

    fiyatlar = get_prices(model)

    # numeric deÄŸeri hesapla ve objeye ekle

@app.route("/about")

    return render_template("about.html")

    app.run(debug=True)

import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

def trendyol_search(query):
    # Arama linki
    url = f"https://www.trendyol.com/sr?q={query}"

    # Bot korumasÄ±na yakalanmamak iÃ§in header
    headers = {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)"
    }

    response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)

    # EÄŸer sayfa gelmediyse boÅŸ dÃ¶ner
    if response.status_code != 200:
        return None

    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser")

    # ÃœrÃ¼n kartlarÄ±nÄ± bul
    items = soup.select("div.p-card-wrppr")

    if not items:
        return None

    # Ä°lk Ã¼rÃ¼nÃ¼ alÄ±yoruz
    first = items[0]

    # ÃœrÃ¼n adÄ±
    title = first.select_one("span.prdct-desc-cntnr-name")
    title = title.get_text(strip=True) if title else "ÃœrÃ¼n bulunamadÄ±"

    # Fiyat
    price = first.select_one("div.prc-box-dscntd")
    if price is None:
        price = first.select_one("div.prc-box-sllng")
    price = price.get_text(strip=True) if price else "Fiyat bulunamadÄ±"

    # Link
    link_tag = first.find("a", href=True)
    if link_tag:
        link = "https://www.trendyol.com" + link_tag["href"]
    else:
        link = None

    return {
        "site": "Trendyol",
        "title": title,
        "price": price,
        "link": link
    }

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from webdriver_manager.chrome import ChromeDriverManager
import time

def trendyol_test_search(query):
    driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=Service(ChromeDriverManager().install()))
    driver.get(f"https://www.trendyol.com/sr?q={query}")

    time.sleep(5)

    # Ä°lk Ã¼rÃ¼nÃ¼n fiyatÄ±nÄ± bulmaya Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±yoruz
    prices = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "div.prc-box-dscntd")

    else:
        print("Fiyat bulunamadÄ±")

    driver.quit()

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from webdriver_manager.chrome import ChromeDriverManager
import time

def trendyol_test_search(query):
    driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=Service(ChromeDriverManager().install()))
    driver.get(f"https://www.trendyol.com/sr?q={query}")

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

driver = webdriver.Chrome()
driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com")

# ğŸ”¹ Ã‡EREZ (varsa)

    cookie = wait.until(EC.element_to_be_clickable(
        (By.ID, "onetrust-accept-btn-handler")
    ))
    cookie.click()
except:
    pass

# ğŸ”¹ ARAMA INPUT (HER SEFERÄ°NDE YENÄ°DEN AL)

    (By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[type='search']")
))

    (By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[type='search']")
))

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time
import re

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

driver = webdriver.Chrome()

search_term = "asus tuf"
search_url = f"https://www.hepsiburada.com/ara?q={search_term.replace(' ', '+')}"
driver.get(search_url)

wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 20)
time.sleep(5)

products = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li[class*='productListContent']")

prices = []

for product in products:
    try:
        price_text = product.find_element(
            By.CSS_SELECTOR,
            "div[data-test-id='price-current-price']"
        ).text

        # "25.999 TL" â†’ 25999
        price_number = int(re.sub(r"\D", "", price_text))
        prices.append(price_number)

    except:
        continue

print("Bulunan fiyat sayÄ±sÄ±:", len(prices))

if prices:
    print("En ucuz fiyat:", min(prices), "TL")
else:
    print("HiÃ§ fiyat bulunamadÄ±")

driver.quit()

from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys

# Arama

    try:
        name = product.find_element(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "h3").text
        price = product.find_element(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "div[data-test-id='price-current-price']").text

        if name and price:
            print(f"{name} â†’ {price}")
            count += 1

    except:
        continue

if count == 0:
    print("HiÃ§ fiyat bulunamadÄ±")

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

service = Service()
driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service)
wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 20)

driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com")

# ğŸ”´ Arama kutusu (doÄŸru selector)
search_box = wait.until(
    EC.element_to_be_clickable((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[type='search']"))
)
search_box.click()
search_box.send_keys("asus tuf")
search_box.send_keys(Keys.ENTER)

# ÃœrÃ¼nlerin yÃ¼klenmesini bekle
wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li.productListContent-item"))
)

products = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li.productListContent-item")

print(f"Bulunan Ã¼rÃ¼n sayÄ±sÄ±: {len(products)}\n")

count = 0

for product in products:
    try:
        name = product.find_element(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "h3").text
        price = product.find_element(
            By.CSS_SELECTOR, "div[data-test-id='price-current-price']"
        ).text

        if name and price:
            print(f"{name} â†’ {price}")
            count += 1

    except:
        continue

if count == 0:
    print("HiÃ§ fiyat bulunamadÄ±")

driver.quit()

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

service = Service()
driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service)
wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 20)

driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com")

# ğŸ”´ Cookie / overlay varsa kapat
try:
    cookie_btn = wait.until(
        EC.element_to_be_clickable((By.ID, "onetrust-accept-btn-handler"))
    )
    cookie_btn.click()
    time.sleep(1)
except:
    pass

# ğŸ”´ Arama input'u bul
search_box = wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[type='search']"))
)

# ğŸ”´ JS ile yaz (click YOK!)

    "arguments[0].value = 'asus tuf';", search_box
)

# ğŸ”´ ÃœrÃ¼nlerin yÃ¼klenmesini bekle

    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li.productListContent-item"))
)

        price = product.find_element(
            By.CSS_SELECTOR, "div[data-test-id='price-current-price']"
        ).text

        print(f"{name} â†’ {price}")
    except:
        continue

driver.quit()

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

service = Service()
driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service)
wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 20)

driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com/ara?q=asus%20tuf")

wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "article"))
)

products = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "article")
print(f"Bulunan Ã¼rÃ¼n kartÄ± sayÄ±sÄ±: {len(products)}\n")

fiyatlar = []

for product in products:
    spans = product.find_elements(By.TAG_NAME, "span")
    for span in spans:
        text = span.text.strip()
        if "TL" in text:
            fiyatlar.append(text)
            print("Bulunan fiyat:", text)
            break  # her Ã¼rÃ¼nden 1 fiyat yeterli

if not fiyatlar:
    print("HiÃ§ fiyat bulunamadÄ±")
else:
    print("\nToplam bulunan fiyat sayÄ±sÄ±:", len(fiyatlar))

driver.quit()

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

driver = webdriver.Chrome()
wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 15)

driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com")

# Ã‡erez / popup bekle (olmazsa geÃ§er)
time.sleep(3)

# Arama kutusu
search_box = wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[aria-label='Site iÃ§inde ara']"))
)

search_box.click()
search_box.send_keys("asus tuf")
search_box.send_keys(Keys.ENTER)

# Arama sonuÃ§larÄ±nÄ±n gelmesini bekle
wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li.productListContent-item"))
)

products = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li.productListContent-item")
print("Bulunan Ã¼rÃ¼n kartÄ± sayÄ±sÄ±:", len(products))

def fiyat_sayiya_cevir(text):
    return int(text.replace(".", "").replace(" TL", ""))

fiyatlar = []

for product in products:
    spans = product.find_elements(By.TAG_NAME, "span")
    for span in spans:
        text = span.text.strip()

        if "TL" in text:
            try:
                fiyat = fiyat_sayiya_cevir(text)
                if fiyat >= 20000:
                    fiyatlar.append(fiyat)
                    print("GerÃ§ek Ã¼rÃ¼n fiyatÄ±:", fiyat, "TL")
                    break
            except:
                pass

if fiyatlar:
    print("\nEn ucuz fiyat:", min(fiyatlar), "TL")
else:
    print("Uygun fiyat bulunamadÄ±")

time.sleep(5)
driver.quit()

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait
from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC
import time
import re

print("Hepsiburada Selenium baÅŸladÄ±")

# Chrome ayarlarÄ±
options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
options.add_argument("--start-maximized")

driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)
wait = WebDriverWait(driver, 15)

# Siteye git
driver.get("https://www.hepsiburada.com")

# Arama kutusu (CLICK YOK!)
search_box = wait.until(
    EC.presence_of_element_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, "input[aria-label='Site iÃ§inde ara']"))
)

search_box.send_keys("asus tuf")
search_box.send_keys(Keys.ENTER)

# ÃœrÃ¼nlerin yÃ¼klenmesini bekle
time.sleep(5)

# ÃœrÃ¼n kartlarÄ±nÄ± bul
product_cards = driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "li[data-test-id='product-card']")
print(f"Bulunan Ã¼rÃ¼n kartÄ± sayÄ±sÄ±: {len(product_cards)}\n")

prices = []

for card in product_cards:
    try:
        price_text = card.text

        # SADECE TL FÄ°YATI YAKALA
        match = re.search(r"(\d{1,3}(\.\d{3})*,\d{2})\s*TL", price_text)

        if match:
            price = match.group(1) + " TL"
            prices.append(price)
            print(f"GerÃ§ek fiyat: {price}")

    except:
        continue

print(f"\nToplam gerÃ§ek fiyat sayÄ±sÄ±: {len(prices)}")

# TarayÄ±cÄ± aÃ§Ä±k kalsÄ±n
input("\nÃ‡Ä±kmak iÃ§in ENTER'a bas...")
driver.quit()
